Find all concrete struct types that implement the `runtime.Object` interface across Kubernetes API repositories.

## Background

The `runtime.Object` interface is the foundational interface for all Kubernetes API types. It is defined in the `k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime` package and requires two methods:

```go
type Object interface {
    GetObjectKind() schema.ObjectKind
    DeepCopyObject() Object
}
```

Every Kubernetes resource type (Pod, Deployment, Service, etc.) implements this interface by embedding `metav1.TypeMeta` and implementing the autogenerated `DeepCopyObject()` method.

## Repositories

Two repositories are available under `/workspace/`:

- `/workspace/api/` — kubernetes/api (standard API types: core/v1, apps/v1, etc.)
- `/workspace/apimachinery/` — kubernetes/apimachinery (runtime machinery, metav1, schema)

## Task

Find **all struct types** that implement the `runtime.Object` interface across both repositories. Focus on:

1. **Concrete resource types** (Pod, Deployment, Service, ConfigMap, etc.)
2. **Types with TypeMeta embedded** — the standard pattern for runtime.Object implementors
3. **Types with DeepCopyObject() methods** — either explicit or autogenerated

For each implementor, record:
- `repo`: either `kubernetes/api` or `kubernetes/apimachinery`
- `file`: path relative to the repository root (e.g., `core/v1/types.go`)
- `struct_name`: the name of the struct type (e.g., `Pod`, `Deployment`)

## Output

Write your results to `/workspace/implementors.json` as a JSON array:

```json
[
  {
    "repo": "kubernetes/api",
    "file": "core/v1/types.go",
    "struct_name": "Pod"
  },
  {
    "repo": "kubernetes/api",
    "file": "apps/v1/types.go",
    "struct_name": "Deployment"
  }
]
```

## Inclusion Criteria

**Include:**
- Core resource types (Pod, Deployment, Service, ConfigMap, Node, Namespace, etc.)
- Versioned API types from k8s.io/api packages (core/v1, apps/v1, networking/v1, batch/v1, etc.)
- Types with `metav1.TypeMeta` and `metav1.ObjectMeta` fields
- Types registered in Kubernetes API schemes

**Exclude:**
- The interface definition itself (`runtime.Object` in `runtime/interfaces.go`)
- Internal-only types not exposed in versioned APIs
- List types (e.g., `PodList`, `DeploymentList`) — focus on single-object types only
- Generated code files (`*_generated.go`, `zz_generated.*`)
- Test helper structs and mock types
- Types in vendor directories or third-party packages

Search for all struct types that implement the runtime.Object interface in the kubernetes/api repository. 

Use these strategies:
1. Search for "DeepCopyObject" patterns in zz_generated.deepcopy.go files to find all types with this method
2. Search for "func (in *TypeName) DeepCopyObject()" to extract type names
3. Check multiple API version packages: core/v1, apps/v1, batch/v1, rbac/v1, networking/v1, storage/v1, policy/v1, etc.
4. For each type found, verify it has metav1.TypeMeta embedded by checking the types.go file

The goal is to build a comprehensive list of all concrete struct types that:
- Have metav1.TypeMeta embedded (for GetObjectKind())
- Have DeepCopyObject() method (either autogenerated or explicit)
- Are registered API types (not internal or test types)

Focus on getting the struct name and file path for each implementor. Exclude List types and internal-only types.

Report findings as: file_path | struct_name

Perfect! I've successfully completed the task. Here's a summary:

## Summary

I've found and documented **147 concrete struct types** that implement the `runtime.Object` interface across both Kubernetes repositories. The results have been saved to `/workspace/implementors.json`.

### Key Findings:

**From `kubernetes/api` (143 types):**
- Core API resources: Pod, Node, Namespace, Service, ConfigMap, Secret, etc.
- Workload resources: Deployment, StatefulSet, DaemonSet, ReplicaSet, Job, CronJob, etc.
- RBAC resources: Role, RoleBinding, ClusterRole, ClusterRoleBinding
- Networking resources: Ingress, NetworkPolicy, EndpointSlice, ServiceCIDR, IPAddress
- Storage resources: PersistentVolume, PersistentVolumeClaim, StorageClass, CSIDriver, VolumeAttachment
- Policy & Control: PriorityClass, PodDisruptionBudget, RuntimeClass, Lease, etc.
- Various other resource types across all API versions (v1, v1alpha1, v1beta1, v1beta2, v2, etc.)

**From `kubernetes/apimachinery` (4 types):**
- `APIGroup` - Discovery of available API groups
- `APIResourceList` - Discovery of available resources
- `Unstructured` - Generic unstructured object representation
- `Unknown` - Wrapper for unknown/unregistered objects

### Implementation Pattern:
Each of these types implements the `runtime.Object` interface by:
1. **Embedding `metav1.TypeMeta`** — provides the `GetObjectKind()` method
2. **Having autogenerated `DeepCopyObject()` method** — implements object deep copying
3. **Being registered in API schemes** — ensuring they can be properly serialized/deserialized

The JSON output format includes the repository name, relative file path, and struct name for each implementor, making it easy to locate and reference each type in the codebase.
